### [42] [VGIF-Score: Interpretable and Diagnostic Evaluation of Spatio-Temporal Instruction Following in Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13527)
*Songyu Xu,Xin Wang,Qiang Chen,Xinran Wang,Muxi Diao,Yuxuan Zhang,Kongming Liang,Rui Lin,Zhanyu Ma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VGIF-Score框架，用于自动、可解释地评估视频生成模型在长且复杂的指令下的遵循能力。该框架包含客观完成度分支（基于时空有向无环图解析指令并进行依赖感知的问答）和主观满意度分支（使用条件化AutoRubric评估影视效果、视觉纯净度、运动流畅性和物理合理性），结合形成统一评分。在包含223个复杂提示和约4300个细粒度评估项的VGIF-Bench基准上，对14个专有及开源视频生成模型进行了超过3000个视频的实验，验证了其可靠性、可解释性和诊断价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成模型评估方法多依赖短而语义浅显的提示，缺乏对原子约束和时空依赖关系的充分考量，且常需人工评估或手工视觉流程，难以提供具体失败原因的诊断信息。因此亟需一种更全面、自动化、可解释的评估框架来衡量模型对复杂指令的理解与执行能力。

Method: 提出VGIF-Score，由两部分组成：(1) 客观完成度分支——将指令解析为时空有向无环图（ST-DAG），进行依赖感知的问答，并支持短路诊断；(2) 主观满意度分支——采用指令条件化的AutoRubric，评估影片质感、视觉纯净度、运动平滑性与物理合理性。两者融合生成综合评分。

Result: 在VGIF-Bench基准上，对14个主流视频生成模型进行测试，结果显示VGIF-Score能有效区分各模型在复杂指令下的表现差异，具备高可靠性、可解释性和诊断能力，显著优于传统评估方式。

Conclusion: VGIF-Score提供了一种高效、自动化且可诊断的视频生成指令遵循评估新范式，推动了对复杂视频生成任务的深入理解与优化。

Abstract: Recent video generation models (VGMs) have made substantial progress in visual fidelity, yet their ability to follow long, compositional instructions remains insufficiently evaluated. Existing evaluation protocols often rely on prompts that are short and semantically shallow, with limited atomic constraints and weak spatio-temporal dependencies. They also frequently depend on costly human evaluation or handcrafted vision pipelines, while providing little diagnostic insight into which instruction constraints succeed or fail. To address this gap, we propose VGIF-Score, a highly automated and interpretable framework for evaluating instruction following in video generation. VGIF-Score consists of two complementary components: an objective completion branch that parses prompts into a Spatio-Temporal Directed Acyclic Graph (ST-DAG) and performs dependency-aware QA with short-circuit diagnostics, and a subjective satisfaction branch that uses instruction-conditioned AutoRubric to assess cinematography, visual purity, motion smoothness, and physics adherence. Together, these components produce a unified score that captures both objective completion and perceptual satisfaction. We instantiate this framework on VGIF-Bench, a benchmark of 223 long, structurally entangled prompts paired with approximately 4.3K fine-grained evaluation items. Experiments on 14 proprietary and open-source VGMs across more than 3K generated videos show that VGIF-Score provides reliable, interpretable, and diagnostically useful evaluation of video generation instruction following. The code will be available at https://github.com/PRIS-CV/VGIF-SCORE.

</details>


### [43] [ThinkBLOX: 3D Indoor Scene Generation with Progressive Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13539)
*Yuan Xiao,Can Wang,Xiangyu Kong,Jing Liao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ThinkBLOX提出一种基于视觉语言模型的渐进式推理框架，通过迭代设计与优化3D场景，解决传统单次生成方法在交互编辑中需全局重优化、布局物理或语义不合理的问题。该框架利用包含20万+样本的ThinkBLOX-Data-200K数据集进行监督微调，并引入分层解耦的强化学习方法Tier-Decoupled GDPO以缓解多目标奖励冲突，显著提升场景的物理合理性、语义一致性与可编辑性，支持全局与局部生成及重排等多种应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于视觉语言模型的3D场景生成方法多采用单次生成范式，导致交互编辑时需全局重优化，且生成布局常存在物理或语义不合理问题，亟需一种能支持渐进式、可交互优化的生成框架。

Method: 提出ThinkBLOX框架，将场景布局生成建模为状态条件下的逐步推理与动作过程；构建ThinkBLOX-Data-200K数据集，包含多视角场景上下文、显式思维链（CoT）和结构化JSON布局；通过监督微调使模型掌握推理与动作间的映射；引入分层解耦的强化学习方法Tier-Decoupled GDPO，分离物理合理性、语义合理性与推理-动作一致性等异构奖励，稳定策略优化。

Result: 实验表明，ThinkBLOX在物理合理性、语义对齐性和交互编辑能力方面显著优于现有单次生成与迭代基线方法；支持多样应用场景，包括全局与局部生成、场景重排等。

Conclusion: ThinkBLOX通过渐进式推理与分层奖励机制，有效解决了3D场景生成中的交互性与布局质量难题，为智能室内场景生成提供了高效、灵活且可扩展的新范式。

Abstract: While traditional graphics methods often synthesize 3D indoor scenes autoregressively or hierarchically, recent vision-language model (VLM)-based generators predominantly adopt a one-shot paradigm where the full layout is planned at once. This one-shot approach often requires global re-optimization or complete reconstruction during interactive editing (e.g., inserting or moving objects) and can lead to physically or semantically poorly organized arrangements. To address these challenges, we propose ThinkBLOX, a VLM-based progressive reasoning framework that iteratively designs and refines 3D scenes. ThinkBLOX treats layout generation as a state-conditioned, step-by-step reasoningand-action process. To power this, we construct the ThinkBLOX-Data-200K dataset, containing 224,757 procedural placement pairs annotated with multi-view scene context, explicit Chain-of-Thought (CoT) rationales, and structured JSON layouts. Through supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on this dataset, the VLM learns to bridge the reasoning-action gap under incremental updates. Furthermore, recognizing that scene synthesis is inherently a multisolution task where SFT suffers from reward conflict, we introduce Tier-Decoupled GDPO. This reinforcement learning scheme organizes heterogeneous rewards into distinct tiers, stabilizing policy optimization across physical validity, semantic plausibility, and reasoning-action consistency. Extensive experiments show that ThinkBLOX significantly outperforms recent one-shot and iterative baselines in physical plausibility, semantic alignment, and interactive editability. Additionally, we show that it supports diverse applications, including both global and local generation and rearrangement of 3D scenes.

### [44] [Nexus: Native Mesh Generation with Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13563)
*Hanxiao Wang,Ying-Tian Liu,Yuan-Chen Guo,Qi-Yuan Feng,Zi-Xin Zou,Ding Liang,Biao Zhang,Yan-Pei Cao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Nexus提出一种基于扩散模型的三角网格生成方法，通过解耦顶点与拓扑生成，实现从粗到细的高质量网格生成。利用八叉树表示稀疏体素化顶点，并采用扩散模型生成顶点；提出Spacetime Interval编码任意边和面拓扑为连续顶点嵌入，实现全局高效拓扑恢复。在Objaverse、Toys4K及真实图像上的实验表明，该方法优于现有自回归和两阶段基线方法，且3D从业者盲测中表现出更强的感知偏好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主流网格生成方法依赖网格序列化和自回归过程，存在推理效率低、误差累积敏感等问题。需要一种更高效、鲁棒的端到端网格生成方法以克服序列建模的固有局限。

Method: 将网格顶点视为八叉树组织的稀疏体素，使用扩散模型进行粗到细的顶点生成；提出Spacetime Interval，将任意边和面拓扑编码为连续顶点嵌入，再通过扩散模型生成嵌入以恢复复杂拓扑结构。

Result: 在Objaverse、Toys4K数据集及真实图像上均显著优于现有自回归和两阶段方法；用户盲测显示3D从业者对生成结果有更强的感知偏好，证明其视觉质量与实用性。

Conclusion: Nexus通过解耦顶点与拓扑生成，结合扩散模型与Spacetime Interval编码，实现了高效、高质量的端到端网格生成，有效克服了传统序列建模的瓶颈，为3D内容创作提供了新范式。

Abstract: Generating high-quality triangle meshes is essential for film, gaming, and interactive 3D applications. Mainstream methods rely on mesh serialization and autoregressive processes, which stuggles in effective inference and is sensitive to error accumulation. In this paper, we present Nexus, a diffusion method that achieves holistic mesh generation via decoupled vertex and topology generation. First, we view mesh vertices as sparse voxels organized as an octree and adopt a diffusion model to generate the vertices in a coarse-to-fine manner. Second, for topology modeling, we propose Spacetime Interval, as an extension of Spacetime Distance to encode arbitrary edge and face topology into continuous per-vertex embeddings. It allows for a global and efficient recovery of complex topology. We then employ a diffusion model to generate the continuous embeddings on the generated vertices. Extensive experiments on the Objaverse and Toys4K datasets and in-the-wild images demonstrate that our method outperforms state-of-the-art autoregressive and two-stage baselines, effectively circumventing the inherent limitations of sequential mesh modeling. A blind user study from 3D practitioners confirms strong perceptual preference for our results.

### [45] [Groc-PO: Grounded Context Preference Optimization for Truthful Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13712)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于人类偏好的对齐方法（如DPO）通常在最终答案层面进行优化，难以直接监督早期视觉定位阶段，导致错误在多阶段推理中传播，影响模型的可信度。

Method: 提出Groc-PO框架，构建GCPD数据集，围绕物体定位、上下文定位和基于上下文的推理三个阶段设计多阶段偏好样本，实现对各阶段的显式偏好监督。

Result: 实验表明，Groc-PO在减少幻觉、提升忠实推理和整体可靠性方面优于标准DPO及其他强基线模型，验证了显式接地监督的有效性。

Abstract: Despite the rapid progress of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), they still suffer from untruthfulness issues, such as visual hallucinations, content fabrication, and unfaithful reasoning, which substantially undermine their faithfulness and practical utility. Alignment methods based on human preference, such as Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), have been widely adopted to address these issues. However, multimodal reasoning errors often propagate across stages, and final-answer errors can often be traced to mistakes in early grounding stages, yet standard DPO typically applies preference optimization at the final-answer level. This credit-assignment challenge means that supervision for early grounding stages is indirect rather than stage-specific, making it difficult to suppress error propagation arising from grounding drift and context inconsistency. To address this, we propose Grounded Context Preference Optimization (Groc-PO), a grounded preference optimization framework for MLLMs. We further construct the Grounded Context Preference Dataset (GCPD), organizing multi-stage preference samples around three stages of Object Grounding, Contextual Grounding, and Grounded Reasoning, to capture the formation, integration, and utilization of grounded context. By introducing more explicit preference supervision over multiple grounded stages, Groc-PO strengthens context-dependent reasoning and mitigates cross-stage error propagation. Extensive experiments show that, compared with standard DPO and other strong baselines, Groc-PO achieves improved performance in hallucination mitigation, faithful reasoning, and overall reliability, supporting the value of more explicit grounded supervision for trustworthy multimodal reasoning.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用边缘-云协同设计：边缘端持续监测车门状态并分割乘客片段；云端VLM基于两阶段粗到精的时空证据优化，识别上车乘客及支付行为。仅对经过视觉定位的乘客片段调用VLM，提高效率与准确性。

Abstract: Transit video understanding can provide valuable fine-grained data that conventional passenger counters and fare systems cannot capture. However, supervised video models require task-specific annotations, while applying vision-language models (VLMs) directly to long onboard videos is unreliable and costly. To leverage the complementary strengths of both approaches, we propose GHR-VLM, a visual grounded hybrid reasoning framework for zero-shot transit-bus video analytics. It is motivated by the observation that explicit visual grounding can improve VLM reasoning by converting long surveillance streams into compact, passenger-centered spatiotemporal evidence. Specifically, we propose an edge-cloud design in which a lightweight edge-based monitor continuously tracks door status and segments passenger clips. A backend VLM then identifies boarding passengers and classifies payment behavior through a two-stage coarse-to-fine refinement of spatiotemporal evidence. By invoking the VLM only on grounded passenger clips and contact sheets, GHR-VLM reduces cloud inference, avoids payment-specific training data, and supplies the localized evidence that VLMs otherwise struggle to identify. Evaluation on 486 minutes of real-world bus surveillance video demonstrates the potential of grounded edge-cloud reasoning for passenger-level payment analytics while highlighting the challenges posed by degraded video conditions.

Abstract: Physically grounded 3D assets are increasingly important for embodied AI and robotic simulation. However, most existing 3D assets lack unified physical semantics, including articulation semantics and intrinsic physical properties, required for realistic interaction. Current approaches either treat these semantics independently or rely on canonicalized object structures, limiting robustness across heterogeneous 3D assets. We present UniPhys, a scalable framework for automatically transforming raw 3D assets into simulation-ready assets with unified physical semantics. Based on UniPhys, we construct UniPhys-40K, a large-scale physically grounded dataset, together with UniPhys-Bench, a carefully verified benchmark for unified physical grounding evaluation. We further introduce UniPhysGen, a unified physical grounding model that jointly reasons over articulation semantics and intrinsic physical properties. UniPhysGen incorporates geometry-robust articulation grounding to mitigate geometric shortcut bias under heterogeneous part decompositions. *Shiyin Lu,Yinglun Li,Yu Xia,Yuhui Chen,An-Yang Ji,Jun-Peng Jiang,Qing-Guo Chen,Jianshan Zhao,En Lin,Haijun Li,Cheng Qin,Zhao Xu,Weihua Luo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OvisOCR2 is a 0.8B end-to-end document parsing model that converts document images into Markdown with natural reading order, supporting text, formulas, tables, and visual regions. It uses a hybrid dataset of real and synthetic documents and employs advanced training techniques including supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning, distillation, and model fusion. It achieves state-of-the-art performance on OmniDocBench v1.6 (96.58) and PureDocBench (75.06), outperforming pipeline methods and demonstrating strong generalization on in-house benchmarks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To develop an end-to-end document parsing model that surpasses traditional pipeline methods by directly generating structured Markdown from document images, improving accuracy, efficiency, and robustness across diverse document types.

Method: OvisOCR2 leverages a data engine combining filtered real-document annotations and synthetically generated pages from HTML sources. Training involves supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning with a multi-component reward on a 4B model, on-policy distillation into the 0.8B model, and model fusion.

Result: OvisOCR2 achieves a state-of-the-art score of 96.58 on OmniDocBench v1.6 and 75.06 Avg3 on PureDocBench, outperforming existing methods. It also demonstrates superior generalization on an in-house benchmark covering long-tail and challenging scenarios.

Conclusion: OvisOCR2 establishes end-to-end document parsing as a competitive alternative to pipeline-based approaches, showing strong performance and robustness across diverse document types, and is publicly available for research and application.

Abstract: We introduce OvisOCR2, a 0.8B document parsing model. OvisOCR2 is designed as an end-to-end parser: given a document page image, it generates a Markdown representation in natural reading order, covering text, formulas, tables, and visual regions. We build a data engine that combines filtered real-document annotations with synthetic pages whose rendered images and Markdown targets are derived from the same HTML source. The training recipe includes supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning on a 4B branch with a multi-component reward design, on-policy distillation into the 0.8B model, and model fusion. On OmniDocBench v1.6, OvisOCR2 achieves a state-of-the-art overall score of 96.58, placing an end-to-end model at the top of this leaderboard previously dominated by pipeline methods and highlighting the potential of end-to-end document parsing. On PureDocBench, OvisOCR2 also achieves the highest Avg3 score of 75.06. Beyond these two public benchmarks, we evaluate OvisOCR2 on an in-house benchmark designed to cover a broader set of long-tail and challenging scenarios. OvisOCR2 obtains the best overall performance among the compared methods, providing further evidence of its generalization and robustness. OvisOCR2 is available at https://huggingface.co/ATH-MaaS/OvisOCR2.

### [49] [Human4K: A Large-Scale 4K Multi-View Mocap Dataset for Whole-Body 3D Human Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13646)
*Tianshun Han,Ziyu Shi,Lijian Liu,Ajian Liu,Benjia Zhou,Hugo Jair Escalante,Yanyan Liang,Sergio Escalera,Zhen Lei,Jun Wan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 3D 人体重建模型在真实世界复杂场景中仍存在几何不稳定、肢体关节不准确、深度模糊或自遮挡下预测不可靠的问题，主要由于缺乏结合高分辨率图像、高精度标注和多样化全身动作的数据集。

Method: 构建 Human4K 数据集，采用八视角高清摄像系统与专业 Vicon 动作捕捉系统同步采集，涵盖 11 名受试者执行复杂、高度关节化且强自遮挡的全身动作；所有序列通过 Motion-Retargeting and Refinement Module (MRRM) 进行姿态精修与对齐，确保全身体态与末端肢体的精确性。

Result: 在标准基准测试上，使用 Human4K 训练的模型表现出一致的性能提升，特别是在手部、脚部以及深度模糊的肢体配置方面取得显著改进。

Conclusion: Human4K 是一个高质量、大规模的多视角全身人体重建数据集，能有效推动 3D 人体重建模型在复杂真实场景下的鲁棒性与精度提升。

Abstract: Recent advances in 3D human reconstruction have improved overall performance, yet current models still fail in the most challenging real-world scenarios. They often produce unstable geometry, inaccurate limb articulation and unreliable predictions under depth ambiguity or self-occlusion. A key reason is that existing datasets still lack the combination of high-resolution images, high-precision annotations and diverse whole-body motions required to support robust reconstruction. To address this gap, we present Human4K, a large-scale 4K multi-view whole-body human reconstruction dataset with mocap-accurate SMPL-X annotations. Human4K contains over six million 4K images captured by an eight-view high-resolution camera system synchronized with a professional Vicon motion capture setup, covering 11 subjects performing complex, highly articulated and strongly self-occluded full-body motions. All sequences are processed by a Motion-Retargeting and Refinement Module (MRRM) to ensure precise alignment for the full body and extremities. Experimental results show that training with Human4K consistently improves whole-body reconstruction on standard benchmarks, with particularly large gains for hands, feet and depth-ambiguous limb configurations.

### [50] [Beyond Color Geometry: Evaluating Human-Like Color Representations in Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13647)
*Ayan Igali,Pakizar Shamoi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于人类感知数据的模糊感知模型，用于评估视觉模型的颜色表征是否与人类相似。该模型包含86个渐进式颜色类别，可衡量类别边界、紧凑性及超越几何空间（如CIELAB）的渐进对齐能力。在11个Vision Transformer模型上测试发现，类别层面表现相近，但渐进对齐差异显著；掩码自编码器（MAE）在超越几何结构的对齐能力上最优，且与其他模型有显著区别。层分析显示，掩码重建过程能保留这种结构。在自然图像中，MAE全局表征表面颜色，而语言监督模型则更关注前景物体的颜色。结果表明，人类色彩理解包含多个独立维度，不应简化为单一指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有颜色表征评估多依赖几何空间（如CIELAB）或离散标签，难以捕捉人类对颜色的渐进式组织方式。本文旨在建立更贴近人类感知的评估框架，揭示视觉模型在颜色理解上的多维特性。

Method: 构建基于86个渐进颜色类别的模糊感知模型，利用人类调查数据拟合。应用于多种视觉编码器，评估三方面属性：类别边界、类别紧凑性、以及超越传统几何空间的渐进对齐能力。通过跨模型比较和层级分析，探究不同架构在颜色表征上的差异。

Result: 所有模型在类别层面表现相近，但在超越几何结构的渐进对齐上差异明显。掩码自编码器（MAE）表现最佳，其置信区间与其他模型无重叠。层分析表明，掩码重建过程有助于保持颜色结构。在自然图像中，MAE倾向于全局表征表面颜色，而语言监督模型更关注对象相关颜色。

Conclusion: 人类色彩感知具有多个独立维度，包括类别边界、紧凑性与渐进对齐等，应避免将这些复杂特征压缩为单一评分。不同视觉模型在这些维度上表现各异，尤其在超越几何表征的能力上存在显著差异。

Abstract: Do vision models see colors the way humans do? Existing evaluations of color representations usually compare them with geometric spaces such as CIELAB or with discrete color labels. These references capture perceptual distance or category membership, but not the graded way in which people organize colors. We evaluate color grounding against a fuzzy perceptual model with 86 graded categories fitted to human survey data. The framework can be applied to any image encoder and measures three complementary properties: category boundaries, category compactness, and graded alignment beyond what color geometry alone can explain. Across eleven Vision Transformer encoders, the category-level results are broadly similar, whereas graded alignment differs substantially. Masked Autoencoders achieve the strongest beyond-geometry alignment, with confidence intervals that do not overlap those of the other encoders. A layer-wise analysis further shows that masked reconstruction preserves this structure toward the output. On natural images, MAE represents surface color globally, while language-supervised models encode color more strongly in relation to the foreground object. These results show that human-like color grounding has several distinct aspects that should not be reduced to a single score.

</details>

*Mohanad Albughdadi*

TL;DR: 该研究针对地球观测数据处理中的可见性预测问题，提出基于LeWorldModel的云感知模型，利用多光谱影像与气象数据预测未来图像是否可用及首次可用时间。模型在23,904个训练片段上训练，具有1800万参数，在多个评估场景中显著优于基线方法（如持久性模型和LightGBM），尤其在连续云量回归和精确恢复时间预测方面表现优异。

Abstract: The bottleneck of Earth Observation processing chains is not the arrival of new imagery but whether the surface is actually visible when the image arrives. We study this as an observability forecasting problem on EarthNet2021. Given recent multispectral imagery and exogenous weather drivers, the goal is to predict whether the next acquisition will be usable and, if not, when a usable view is likely to return. To do this, we adapt LeWorldModel, a joint-embedding predictive architecture world model, to cloud-aware Earth Observation sequences. The final pipeline converts raw minicubes into episodic HDF5 sequences with five image channels (blue, green, red, near-infrared, cloud mask) and eight meteorological and calendar covariates. The resulting model has 18.0M trainable parameters and is trained from scratch on 23,904 training episodes. The trained leWorldModel is evaluated under a locked protocol: linear probes are fit on train only, calibration choices are set on an internal validation split, and the fitted heads are then frozen for valsplit, IID, OOD, and extreme evaluation. On the full frozen-bundle observability benchmark, LeWorldModel consistently outperforms persistence. For next-step usability, balanced accuracy ranges from 0.769 to 0.887, compared with 0.493 to 0.556 for persistence. For exact first-usable-horizon prediction, accuracy ranges from 0.602 to 0.806, compared with 0.120 to 0.369 for persistence. Against a frozen LightGBM baseline fit on the same training windows, LeWorldModel is better on continuous clear/cloud regression and on exact recovery timing on valsplit, IID, and extreme, while LightGBM is stronger on the simpler binary any-usable-within-six task and is more robust on OOD. In separate sampled diagnostic analyses, LeWM also produces strong ranking-based anomaly signals under synthetic temporal inconsistencies.

### [52] [Exploratory, Communicative, and Deployable: Vision-Driven Embodied Agents for Open-World Mobile Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13653)
*Boyu Mi,Mengchen Ma,Yifei Yao,Xing Gao,Junting Chen,Yangzi Li,Zihou Zhu,Guohao Li,Zhenfei Yin,Tai Wang,Yao Mu,Jiangmiao Pang,Hanqing Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: REAL 是一个用于开放世界移动操作的代理框架，通过模拟用户实现人机交互，设计多样化任务以驱动数据收集和训练，引入 REAL-Bench 基准评估性能。实验表明，该框架在交互任务中超越领先商业 VLMs，物理机器人上实现 78.3% 的端到端成功率，验证了其在未见家庭场景中的零样本迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有框架依赖模拟器特权状态或完整指令，无法应对真实部署挑战。需要一种能支持主动探索、视觉定位和交互意图消歧的开放世界移动操作框架。

Method: 构建 sim-to-real 一致的环境接口，不依赖感知真值；集成模拟用户实现人机交互；设计多样任务组合用于数据收集、监督微调与在线强化学习；采用分层训练流程优化工具使用能力和开放词汇推理。

Result: 在交互任务中成功率达到 56.9%，显著优于领先商业 VLMs；物理机器人在 60 次真实任务中实现 78.3% 的端到端成功率，表现出强大的零样本迁移能力。

Conclusion: REAL 框架通过模拟用户与一致环境设计有效弥合了仿真与现实之间的差距，实现了长时程移动操作的鲁棒真实部署，具备在未见场景中良好泛化的能力。

Abstract: Real-world deployment of embodied agents requires active exploration, visual grounding, and interactive intent disambiguation. However, existing frameworks often rely on privileged simulator states or assume complete instructions, bypassing realistic deployment challenges. To bridge this gap, we present REAL, an agentic framework for open-world mobile manipulation. REAL establishes sim-to-real-consistent environment APIs without oracle perception and integrates a simulated user to enable human-in-the-loop interaction. Within this environment, we design diverse task compositions to drive data collection, supervised fine-tuning, and online reinforcement learning, systematically optimizing agent performance. To comprehensively evaluate this approach, we introduce REAL-Bench, a benchmark spanning 241 tasks across active exploration, visual distraction, articulated manipulation, and interactive disambiguation.
  Experimental results demonstrate that our trained agent outperforms leading commercial closed-source VLMs on interactive tasks with a 56.9% success rate. Further empirical analysis reveals that our hierarchical training pipeline successfully aligns the model's tool-use capabilities while maintaining robust open-vocabulary reasoning under extended exploration horizons. Finally, we deploy and evaluate our framework on a physical dual-arm mobile robot, where it achieves a 78.3% end-to-end success rate over 60 real-world episodes. These physical trials demonstrate robust zero-shot transferability to unseen household scenarios, validating that our sim-to-real-consistent design successfully bridges the reality gap for long-horizon mobile manipulation. Code is available at https://github.com/InternRobotics/REAL.

### [53] [T3HG-Editor: Text-driven 3D Human Garment Editing with Body Priors Embedded in SMPL-X](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13654)
*Shaoru Sun,Xingtao Wang,Zihan Ma,Wenrui Li,Jiantao Zhou,Debin Zhao,Xiaopeng Fan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: T3HG-Editor包含三个阶段：1）沿SMPL-X法线播种高斯点并结合2D掩码精确定位待编辑高斯；2）跨视图聚合同一顶点对应标记并回传至原视图，实现无额外训练的服装一致性约束；3）利用SMPL-X定义的有符号距离函数（SDF）构建人体距离场，结合2D语义掩码修剪溢出高斯，防止非目标区域污染。

Abstract: While 3D Gaussian Editing (3DGE) has seen substantial progress, text-driven 3D human garment editing remains largely underexplored. Extending such methods to 3D human garment editing suffers from low-fidelity outcomes, caused by introduced distortions and garment inconsistencies. Motivated by this insight, we propose a text-driven 3D human garment editor termed T3HG-Editor, which delivers high-fidelity and garment consistent results by leveraging geometry and joint priors embedded in SMPL-X. Specifically, T3HG-Editor contains three stages, namely obtainment of editable Gaussians, garment consistent editing, and Gaussian updating with overflow pruning. The obtainment of editable Gaussians begins with seeding Gaussians along SMPL-X normals to generate sufficient near surface Gaussians, followed by a 2D mask constraint that precisely localizes the target Gaussians to be edited. The garment consistent editing aggregates tokens corresponding to the same SMPL-X vertex across multiple views and propagates them to their original views, enforcing garment consistency without requiring additional training. Gaussian updating with overflow pruning employs a Signed Distance Function (SDF) defined on SMPL-X to construct a human distance field, which is then integrated with a 2D semantic mask to prune overflowing Gaussians, thus preventing contamination of non-target regions. Experiments on multiple subjects and diverse garment types demonstrate that T3HG-Editor outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both editing quality and garment consistency.

Nevertheless, this data is costly and fails to scale, which is essential for accurate light-source-level control. Conversely, inverse-rendering methods reduce the data dependency by incorporating physical priors; however, they lack the robustness of intrinsic estimation in challenging conditions.
  In this paper, we present FreeLit, a paired-free framework for controllable indoor relighting that explicitly manipulates light-source location, color, and intensity. Instead of relying on paired supervision, we construct a physics-guided illumination prior from intrinsic scene properties, generating a structured lightmap along with a pseudo-relit image to guide diffusion-based synthesis. To address instability in intrinsic estimation, especially in low-light scenes, we introduce a relighting-guided intrinsic stabilization strategy that enforces illumination-invariant reflectance through structure-aware distillation and consistency constraints. Furthermore, we propose controllability-oriented evaluation metrics to quantify alignment with user-specified illumination color and intensity. Experimental results demonstrate that FreeLit achieves stable, physically consistent, and controllable relighting, with improved robustness in low-light indoor scenes, without requiring paired supervision.

### [57] [WAVE-Stereo: Warp-Aligned Volume Encoding for Stereo Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13674)
*Zehan Liu,Yage He,Xianwu Gong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: WAVE-Stereo提出了一种新的立体匹配方法，通过将相关体积和特征扭曲作为互补的匹配线索，在ConvGRU输入中并行编码匹配搜索、残差对齐和视差先验。为解决无纹理区域的匹配退化问题，引入周期性全局上下文传播（PGCP）。在多个真实世界基准测试中，WAVE-Stereo实现了具有竞争力的零样本泛化性能，同时保持高效推理速度，表现出良好的精度与效率平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有迭代立体匹配方法分别建模相关体积和特征扭曲，但二者未有效结合。本文旨在利用两者提供的互补匹配线索，提升匹配精度，尤其在纹理缺失区域的鲁棒性。

Method: 提出GeoWarp Correspondence Encoder（GWCE）以并行处理匹配搜索、残差对齐和视差先验；引入周期性全局上下文传播（PGCP）增强无纹理区域的上下文信息传递。

Result: 在Middlebury、ETH3D、KITTI 2012、KITTI 2015和Booster五个基准上实现优异的零样本泛化性能：KITTI 2015上达到3.18% D1-all，Booster上达到4.42% Bad-2.0，推理时间仅66ms，兼具高精度与实时性。

Conclusion: WAVE-Stereo通过融合相关体积与特征扭曲的互补信息，并引入周期性全局上下文传播，显著提升了立体匹配在复杂场景下的准确性和鲁棒性，为实时高精度立体匹配提供了新范式。

Abstract: Existing iterative stereo matching methods primarily adopt two types of correspondence representation: explicit matching search via correlation volumes and local residual refinement via warped features, yet the two remain separately modeled. We propose WAVE-Stereo, built on a core insight: correlation volumes and feature warping provide complementary matching cues. \textbf{GeoWarp Correspondence Encoder (GWCE)} encodes matching search, residual alignment, and disparity prior in parallel at the ConvGRU input. To mitigate matching degradation in textureless regions, we propose \textbf{Periodic Global Context Propagation (PGCP)}, which propagates global spatial information in a periodic manner. On five real-world benchmarks -- Middlebury, ETH3D, KITTI 2012, KITTI 2015, and Booster -- WAVE-Stereo achieves competitive zero-shot generalization accuracy without any external foundation model prior, achieving 3.18\% D1-all on KITTI 2015, 4.42\% Bad-2.0 on Booster, and 66ms real-time inference, striking a favorable balance between accuracy and efficiency. Our code is available at https://github.com/yamanoko-do/WAVE-Stereo.

### [58] [Towards Spatial Supersensing in the Wild](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13681)

Abstract: Humans can efficiently parse continuous sensory streams, from hours to years, scaffolding an internal world model that grounds spatial reasoning and prediction. Notably, inspired by cognitive studies on how humans structure experience, we systematically probe the full triad of world state: the agent (observer), objects (scene items), and the environment (places and global layout). In total, VSI-Super-Wild contains $\textbf{6,980}$ human-verified question-answer pairs derived from $\textbf{442}$ real-world videos spanning 8 scene categories, including long-form recordings exceeding 4 hours. Results on VSI-Super-Wild expose a fundamental disconnect: despite advances in static image understanding, models consistently fail at tasks that require coherent world-state tracking over time. We characterize how performance degrades with world-state complexity and temporal horizon, and diagnose four failure modes: spatial collapse, semantic shortcuts, insufficient update, and instance confusion. This taxonomy reveals that models lack mechanisms to bind objects, agents, and environments into a unified spatial world model, a fundamental gap that defines the path forward for spatial supersensing.

### [59] [Calibrated Closed-Form Uncertainty for Radiative Gaussian Splatting in Sparse-View CT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13682)
*Chulin Zhao,Yiran Xu,Shu Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于辐射高斯点云的CT重建方法，通过利用透射X射线成像中投影与体素化过程的线性特性，为高斯密度引入可变的后验分布，实现预测方差在体积空间和投影空间中的精确闭式传播。该方法在单次前向传播中完成不确定性计算，并首次系统地进行了高斯点云CT的校准研究，结果显示其每体素不确定性能有效排名真实重建误差，在14/15场景中表现优异，且经温度缩放后9个场景达到幅度校准目标。相比之下，现有扰动集成方法在相同条件下表现较差（相关性低至-0.08）。进一步分析揭示了三种视图采集模式：平坦、病态和各向异性，表明仅在各向异性情况下，基于不确定性的主动采样才能带来显著优势。因此提出了覆盖门控、成熟度调度的采集策略，并指出该方法可支持剂量自适应停止规则，但实验验证留待未来工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于辐射高斯点云的CT重建方法虽快速，但仅输出点估计，缺乏对重建可信度的量化表示。由于传统RGB点云无法保证投影与体素化的线性关系，而透射X射线成像具备此性质，本文旨在利用这一特性，构建具有可解释不确定性的高斯点云模型，以提升重建结果的可靠性与可信赖性。

Method: 利用透射X射线成像中投影与体素化操作的线性特性，建立高斯密度的变分后验分布，推导出体积空间和投影空间中预测方差的闭式表达式（σ²(x) = ∑g_i(x)²s_i² 与 Var[I_p] = ∑w_{i,p}²s_i²），并通过温度缩放进行不确定性校准。采用系统性校准评估（Spearman / AUSE / ECE）验证性能，并设计覆盖门控与成熟度调度的主动视图选择策略，探索剂量自适应停止机制。

Result: 所提方法在14/15个官方基准场景中成功将不确定性排名与真实误差对齐，其中9个场景经温度缩放后满足幅度校准要求；而对比方法（扰动集成）相关性极低（最低-0.08）。控制实验表明，不确定性驱动的视图选择仅在各向异性场景中具有明显优势，支持设计覆盖感知的采集策略，并为剂量自适应停止提供理论基础。

Conclusion: 本研究首次实现了高斯点云在CT重建中高效、精确的不确定性建模，具备良好的校准性和可解释性。通过系统分析不同采集场景下的不确定性行为，提出覆盖门控与成熟度调度的主动采集策略，为未来智能、低剂量、自适应的CT扫描系统奠定了方法基础。

Abstract: Radiative Gaussian splatting has made sparse-view CT reconstruction fast, but existing methods output point estimates with no notion of where the reconstruction can be trusted. We exploit a property of transmissive X-ray imaging that RGB splatting cannot claim -- projection and voxelization are strictly linear in the per-Gaussian densities -- to equip radiative Gaussians with a variational density posterior whose predictive variance propagates in closed form, exactly, in a single forward pass, in both volume space ($σ^2(x)=\sum_i g_i(x)^2 s_i^2$) and projection space ($\mathrm{Var}[I_p]=\sum_i w_{i,p}^2 s_i^2$). We present the first systematic calibration study for Gaussian-splatting CT (Spearman / AUSE / ECE with temperature scaling), showing that the resulting per-voxel uncertainty ranks true reconstruction error on 14 of 15 scenes of the official benchmark across three view budgets -- 9 of 15 additionally meeting our magnitude-calibration target after a single temperature -- while the perturbation-ensemble heuristic of concurrent work, transplanted to voxel space under the same protocol on our development scenes, does not (rank correlation as low as $-0.08$). We then dissect why uncalibrated acquisition scores can nevertheless select acceptable views, identifying three regimes -- flat (isotropic, balanced), pathological (degenerate coverage), and anisotropic -- and showing, in controlled single-scene testbeds, that principled uncertainty earns a measurable premium only in the last, motivating a coverage-gated, maturity-scheduled acquisition policy; the same calibrated posterior further points toward a dose-adaptive stopping rule, whose experimental validation we leave to future work.

</details>


### [60] [DNA: Dual-stage Native Attribution for Generated Image Source Tracing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13685)
*Chao Wang,Kejiang Chen,Zijin Yang,Yaofei Wang,Yuang Qi,Weiming Zhang,Nenghai Yu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DNA框架，通过双阶段（粗粒度+细粒度）分析生成模型的潜在层次特征，实现无需额外训练的源模型归属。利用自编码器双重重建（AEDR）进行家族级筛选，再通过原生预测一致性（NPC）在噪声和语义条件下区分同家族不同变体，显著提升准确率。构建DNA-30K基准数据集用于开放集评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主动方法依赖水印或模型修改，影响图像质量且部署受限；被动方法依赖大规模监督学习或单一重建信号，难以处理未知来源及高度相似的同家族变体。

Method: 提出双阶段天然归属（DNA）框架：第一阶段使用Autoencoder Double-Reconstruction（AEDR）进行高效开放集家族级筛选；第二阶段采用Native Prediction Consistency（NPC），通过多噪声水平下语义条件化的原生预测误差比较，计算归一化校准得分以实现模型级归属。

Result: 在DNA-30K基准上，DNA实现89.11%的端到端归属准确率，远超随机猜测（<1%）；相比最强基线提升33.81%，即使在使用AEDR作为粗粒度阶段时仍表现优异。

Conclusion: DNA框架利用生成模型潜空间的分层特性，无需额外训练即可有效实现同家族变体的源模型归属，在开放集场景下具备高精度与强泛化能力。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of image generation has produced numerous within-family variants, making source-model attribution of suspect images increasingly important for digital forensics. Existing proactive methods rely on watermark embedding or model modification, which may degrade visual quality and limit deployment flexibility. Passive methods often rely on large-scale supervised training or a single reconstruction signal, limiting their ability to handle unknown sources and distinguish highly similar within-family variants. We observe that attribution signals in latent generative models are naturally stratified across architectural levels: VAE-level cues reflect family-shared information, whereas backbone-level cues capture variant-specific behaviors. Motivated by this insight, we propose Dual-stage Native Attribution (DNA), a coarse-to-fine framework that follows this hierarchy without additional neural-network training. The coarse-grained stage uses Autoencoder Double-Reconstruction (AEDR) for efficient open-set family-level screening. The fine-grained stage performs closed-set model-level attribution with Native Prediction Consistency (NPC), which compares native prediction errors of within-family variants across multiple noise levels under semantic conditioning and attributes the source via normalized calibrated scores. To enable systematic evaluation, we construct DNA-30K, a benchmark for within-family variant attribution under open-set family-level evaluation. It comprises 30,000 images generated by 24 candidate models across six families spanning both denoising diffusion and flow matching, plus non-candidate generated and natural images as unknown sources. Experiments show that DNA achieves 89.11% end-to-end attribution accuracy on a task where random guessing accuracy is below 1% and outperforms the strongest baseline by 33.81% even when AEDR is used as the coarse-grained stage.

</details>


### [61] [Barnamala: Parameter-Efficient Handwritten Devanagari Recognition at Benchmark Saturation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13689)
*Ashish Thapa,Samrat Karki*

Conclusion: 模型性能已接近理论极限，小型网络在精度、效率与鲁棒性方面全面超越大型模型，证明了紧凑架构的潜力。

Abstract: We built a compact convolutional network (1.11 M parameters) for 46-class DHCD Devanagari recognition and reached 99.73%, the highest reported at 15.6x smaller than prior state-of-the-art. We have effectively reached the saturation point: every model tested, large teacher ensembles included, hits the same 11-error intrinsic floor. No configuration achieves a statistically clear win under exact McNemar tests with Wilson confidence intervals. Even without knowledge distillation, our student matches the nearest large-model baseline (17.32 M parameters; McNemar $p = 0.345$). Outside of DHCD, zero-shot on CMATERdb digits gives 76.6% and fine-tuning reaches 97.8%; corruption robustness is also far better than large baselines (mean corruption accuracy 75.7% vs. 38.7%). ### [62] [Anatomically Faithful but Temporally Blind: Auditing Attribution for Left-Ventricular Ejection-Fraction Estimation from Echocardiography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13738)
*Hyunkyung Han,Min Jung Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究评估了深度视频模型在超声心动图中估算左心室射血分数（EF）时的解释性，发现尽管模型在空间上能准确聚焦左心室，但在时间上对关键的收缩末期（ES）和舒张末期（ED）帧缺乏敏感性，说明空间忠实性不能保证时间忠实性。使用多种归因方法与消融实验验证后发现，模型实际并未依赖临床关键帧，表明现有解释技术可能掩盖模型的时间盲点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度学习模型在超声心动图中估算左心室射血分数（EF）已达到近专家水平，但其决策过程的可解释性仍需验证。特别是，基于后处理归因方法（如Chefer、Grad-CAM）虽能显示模型关注区域，但无法确认其是否真正依赖临床关键的收缩末期（ES）和舒张末期（ED）帧。因此，亟需系统评估解释的时空忠实性，以确保XAI用于模型验证的可靠性。

Method: 研究在EchoNet-Dynamic数据集上微调两种不同架构的EF回归模型：自监督的VideoMAE Transformer 和 基于Kinetics预训练的R(2+1)D CNN。采用与其架构匹配的归因方法（如Chefer for Transformer，Grad-CAM for CNN），从三个维度评估解释的忠实性：空间上的交并比（IoR）与左心室掩码的对比，删除法的AUC，以及针对ES/ED帧的时间定位指数。所有指标均相对于随机水平进行比较，并计算50例样本的95%置信区间。此外，通过管状遮蔽探针（tubelet-occlusion probe）区分归因失败与模型真实行为。

Result: 两个模型在空间上均表现出显著的忠实性（VideoMAE的IoR为基准的2.91倍，R(2+1)D为1.98倍），但时间定位能力与随机水平无显著差异（0.97–1.00倍），表明模型未有效识别关键帧。遮蔽实验进一步显示，模型并未偏好使用ES/ED帧（仅为基准的0.90倍），说明时间盲点源于模型本身的行为，而非归因方法的偏差。

Conclusion: 空间忠实性并不等同于时间忠实性。现有的可解释性方法可能在确认模型“看对位置”的同时，掩盖其忽略临床关键帧的问题。这警示我们，在使用XAI验证视频诊断模型时必须引入时间感知的训练与评估机制，以确保模型真正依赖正确的临床信息。

Abstract: Background and Objective: Deep video models estimate left-ventricular ejection fraction (EF) from echocardiography with near-expert accuracy, and post-hoc attribution (Chefer relevance for transformers, Grad-CAM for CNNs) is increasingly used to certify that models "look at the right place." Yet whether these explanations are faithful both spatially and temporally is unaudited. Because EF is defined by the end-systolic (ES) and end-diastolic (ED) frames, a faithful explanation must localize the left ventricle (space) and the decisive frames (time).
  Methods: We fine-tune two distinct EF regressors on EchoNet-Dynamic -- a self-supervised VideoMAE transformer and a Kinetics-pretrained R(2+1)D CNN -- and audit each with architecture-matched attribution along three axes: intersection-over-relevance (IoR) against LV masks, deletion AUC, and a temporal localization index on ES/ED frames, each relative to chance with per-case 95% CIs over 50 studies. A tubelet-occlusion probe separates attribution failure from model behavior.
  Results: Both models are anatomically faithful -- IoR 2.91x (VideoMAE) and 1.98x (R(2+1)D) above chance -- yet temporally blind: temporal localization is indistinguishable from chance (0.97--1.00) and no better than random attribution. Occlusion shows the models do not preferentially rely on ES/ED (0.90x chance), so temporal blindness reflects model behavior, not an attribution artifact.
  Conclusions: Spatial faithfulness does not imply temporal faithfulness. Attribution can certify anatomical grounding while masking that a model ignores the clinically decisive frames -- a caution for XAI-based validation of video diagnostic models and a call for temporally-aware training and evaluation.

</details>

These results show that prospective Indication is strongly associated with report-derived targets, permutation-aware fusion is competitive, and post-hoc report text creates substantial report-label circularity.

### [65] [RainDancer: RGB-Event Video Deraining with Rain-Oriented Spiking Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13802)
*Kui Jiang,Runzhe Li,Zhaocheng Yu,Guanglu Sun,Junjun Jiang,Xianming Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RainDancer是一种基于先分解后交互范式的渐进式RGB-事件视频去雨框架，通过在每个模态内分离雨和背景成分，再进行组件级融合，有效缓解跨模态干扰。该方法在RGB分支中逐步分解帧特征为雨与背景表示，在事件分支中采用面向雨的脉冲神经网络模块捕捉与雨运动相关的稀疏爆发性事件动态，并引入事件域监督以正则化稀疏事件重建、结构一致性和梯度方向。在合成与真实数据集上的实验表明，该方法在定量指标、视觉质量及下游感知鲁棒性方面均表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于RGB序列的去雨方法在动态雨景中因雨痕、纹理、边界、运动和遮挡等视觉模式相似而存在歧义；虽然事件相机提供高时间分辨率的运动敏感线索，但其事件流包含传感器噪声和背景触发响应，直接进行RGB-事件融合易引入跨模态干扰。因此，亟需一种能有效解耦雨与背景成分并实现精准跨模态融合的方法。

Method: 提出RainDancer框架，采用‘分解-交互’范式：在RGB分支中逐级分解帧特征为雨与背景表示；在事件分支中设计雨导向的脉冲神经网络模块，提取与雨运动相关的稀疏爆发事件动态；随后对语义对齐的组件进行融合，以保持结构并抑制雨；同时引入事件域监督，约束稀疏事件重建、结构一致性与梯度方向。

Result: 在合成与真实RGB-事件视频去雨数据集上，RainDancer在定量指标（如PSNR、SSIM）、视觉质量以及下游任务（如目标检测、跟踪）的鲁棒性方面均优于现有方法，验证了其有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: RainDancer通过模态内成分分解与组件级融合，有效解决了RGB-事件跨模态融合中的干扰问题，显著提升了复杂动态雨景下的去雨性能，为多模态视频恢复提供了新思路。

Abstract: Video deraining aims to recover clean visual content from rainy videos for reliable perception under adverse weather. Existing methods mainly rely on RGB sequences and temporal redundancy, but RGB-only restoration remains ambiguous in dynamic rainy scenes, where rain streaks, textures, boundaries, motion, and occlusions may share similar visual patterns. Event cameras provide complementary motion-sensitive cues with high temporal resolution, but event streams also contain sensor noise and background-triggered responses, so direct RGB-Event fusion may introduce cross-modal interference. To address this issue, we propose RainDancer, a progressive RGB-Event video deraining framework based on a decompose-before-interact paradigm. The core idea is to separate rain and background components within each modality before cross-modal interaction. In the RGB branch, frame features are progressively decomposed into rain and background representations. In the event branch, a rain-oriented spiking neural network module captures sparse and bursty event dynamics associated with rain motion. Component-level fusion is then performed between semantically aligned representations for structure preservation and rain suppression. We further introduce event-domain supervision to regularize sparse event reconstruction, structural consistency, and gradient orientation. Experiments on synthetic and real RGB-Event video deraining datasets demonstrate superior quantitative performance, visual quality, and downstream perception robustness. Code is available at https://github.com/AE86-plus/RainDancer.

### [66] [AspectCLIP: Optimizing CLIP Representation Space via Aspect-Guided Consistency Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13805)
*Yiyang Yao,Shanglin Liu,Jianming Lv,Chengjun Wang,Jinyi Li,Yuchan Jie,Zhihua Jin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AspectCLIP提出一种新的对比学习框架，通过考虑图像与文本间的信息不对称性（即一个图像可对应多种不同描述），将训练样本按文本相似性聚类为语义一致的组，并在组内实施完整的循环一致性约束，而跨组则仅在原型层面进行比较。该方法有效避免了传统全局正则化带来的语义扭曲，提升了表示空间的结构化程度，在下游任务中表现优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对比语言-图像预训练方法忽略图像与文本间的信息不对称性：同一图像可能有多个完全不同描述的文本，导致全局一致性正则化错误地约束视觉相似但语义不同的图像对，引入语义偏差。

Method: AspectCLIP首先基于文本相似性对训练样本进行属性聚类，识别出描述相同方面的语义一致组；然后在每个组内施加完整的循环一致性约束，而跨组间的正则化仅限于原型级别的比较，从而实现对特定语义方面的一致性强化，同时保持跨方面的灵活性。

Result: 实验表明，AspectCLIP在多个下游任务上均优于传统方法，且学习到的表示空间更具结构性，有效缓解了因全局正则化导致的语义扭曲问题。

Conclusion: AspectCLIP通过引入基于语义方面的分组与层次化正则化机制，成功应对了图像-文本信息不对称带来的挑战，显著提升了对比学习中表示空间的质量与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Contrastive Language-Image Pretraining learns a shared representation space through large-scale contrastive learning. However, existing methods that enforce global consistency regularization overlook a key challenge: the inherent information asymmetry between images and text: captions typically describe only one specific aspect of an image, thus images with similar visual content can be paired with completely divergent textual content and semantic information. Consequently, global regularizers inadvertently impose constraints between visually similar images whose captions describe divergent aspects, introducing semantic distortion into the representation space. We propose AspectCLIP, a framework that reformulates consistency regularization to respect this one-to-many structure. AspectCLIP first partitions training samples into attribute clusters based on textual similarity to identify aspect-coherent groups, then applies full cyclic consistency within each cluster while restricting cross-cluster regularization to prototype-level comparisons. This aspect-guided regularization enforces strict geometric alignment only when images and texts describe a consistent facet, while allowing flexibility across divergent aspects. Extensive experiments on downstream tasks demonstrate that AspectCLIP consistently outperforms traditional methods and achieves a more structured representation space.

</details>


### [67] [Bake It Till You Make It: Ultrafast Spatial Texture-Atlas Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13808)
*Neel Kelkar,Simon Niedermayr,Kaloian Petkov,Klaus Engel,Rüdiger Westermann*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种解耦的辐射表示方法，通过2D surfels建模低频几何和视图相关外观特征，并利用视图无关的空间哈希网格以紧凑纹理贴图形式存储高频纹理。结合稀疏性优化策略，有效剪枝不显著的surfels，实现比以往方法更快、更稀疏的重建。利用几何稀疏性和高效的GPU纹理映射，该方法在保持顶级视觉保真度的同时，实现了高达5倍的速度提升，可在消费级硬件上实现4K实时60帧渲染。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D高斯溅射（3DGS）方法虽能捕捉精细颜色细节，但依赖基于哈希网格的外观参数化导致片段渲染计算成本高，亟需降低计算开销同时保持高质量渲染。

Method: 采用解耦的辐射表示：使用2D surfels表示低频几何与视图相关的外观特征；用视图无关的空间哈希网格存储高频纹理，并将其烘焙为紧凑纹理贴图；引入惩罚半透明性和每原始体衰减的稀疏性增强优化，以主动剪枝无效surfels。

Result: 相比传统3DGS方法，本方法在保持状态领先视觉质量的前提下，实现了最高达五倍的渲染速度提升，支持在消费级硬件上实现实时4K 60FPS渲染。

Conclusion: 该方法通过解耦表示与稀疏性优化，在保证高质量渲染的同时显著提升了效率，为实时3D内容生成与渲染提供了高效可行的新方案。

Abstract: Recent extensions of 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) capture fine color details using hash-grid-based appearance parameterization but incur high computational cost during fragment rendering. We introduce a decoupled radiance representation that models low-frequency geometry and view dependent appearance features with 2D surfels while representing high-frequency textures via a view-independent spatial hash grid that is baked into a compact texture atlas. By including sparsity-enhancing optimizations that penalize semi-transparency and per-primitive falloff, our method aggressively prunes insignificant surfels and achieves significantly faster and sparser reconstructions than prior work. Exploiting geometric sparsity and efficient GPU texture mapping, our approach achieves up to a fivefold speedup over 3DGS while preserving state-of-the-art visual fidelity, enabling real-time 4K rendering at 60 FPS on consumer hardware.

</details>

Conclusion: 所提出的多模态深度学习框架在胰腺癌可切除性评估中表现优异，能够实现自动化、高精度分类，有助于提高临床决策的一致性和效率。

Abstract: Accurate determination of pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma (PDAC) resectability relies on evaluating how the tumor interacts with major peripancreatic vessels on CT imaging, yet expert assessment often shows substantial variability. The approach uses a Swin-UNETR backbone to obtain anatomy aware image representations through auxiliary segmentation of pancreas, tumor, and vascular structures. These features are fused with a compact clinical embedding derived from 17 routinely collected variables and processed by a lightweight classification head. Model training is guided by a dynamic multitask objective that adapts the balance between segmentation and classification based on current tumor Dice performance, promoting feature representations that remain both anatomically informed and discriminative.

Abstract: While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated remarkable success in 2D medical image understanding, their extension to 3D volumetric imaging remains hindered by prohibitive annotation costs and dataset opacity. To address this limitation, we introduce a large-scale structured reasoning dataset constructed via a novel slice-wise data synthesis paradigm. To validate this approach, we instruction-tune a standard 2D-pretrained MLLM baseline using the synthesized data to enhance its volumetric comprehension. Comprehensive evaluations across multiple 3D medical benchmarks demonstrate that our method yields significant performance improvements over the 2D baseline. Furthermore, the resulting model exhibits robust spatial reasoning capabilities and rivals resource-intensive native 3D architectures, effectively bridging the performance gap. Ultimately, this data-centric strategy unlocks deep volumetric understanding and highly interpretable clinical logic without requiring computationally expensive 3D-specific pre-training. The complete repository, including datasets and training workflows, is publicly available at https://github.com/2020420145009/hounsfield.

Abstract: Human-object interaction detection (HOID) has traditionally been formulated as a supervised detection problem over predefined interaction categories. While such paradigms achieve strong performance on closed-set benchmarks, they fundamentally entangle interaction understanding with dataset-specific supervision, limiting their ability to generalize to open-world and compositional scenarios. Recent HOI detectors attempt to leverage MLLMs through prompting strategies to transfer interaction-specific knowledge. However, such prompt-based approaches primarily focus on extracting discriminative representations from pretrained models, while underexploring their inherent multimodal reasoning capabilities. As a result, they struggle to provide informative contextual reasoning for ambiguous and open-world interaction scenarios. In this work, we present AgentHOI, a training-free, agentic framework that transfers the generalist multimodal reasoning capabilities of foundation models to HOI detection in the wild. Instead of learning interaction classifiers, AgentHOI modularly orchestrates complementary vision foundation modules to perform open-ended semantic reasoning and spatial grounding in a coordinated manner. To address the challenges of incomplete interaction discovery and ambiguous localization in complex scenes, we introduce two key mechanisms: (1) Context-aware Multi-round Reasoning, which progressively refines interaction hypotheses to ensure exhaustive and compositional HOI discovery, and (2) Multifaceted Interaction Localization, which enhances grounding precision by generating instance-specific descriptions that integrate semantic, spatial, and appearance cues. ### [71] [Fine-Grained Vision-Language Pretraining with Organ-Conditioned Pattern Tokens for CT Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13892)
*Guoliang You,Xiaomeng Chu*

Main category: cs.CV

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: OCP-CT保留了一个稳定的全局CT-报告对比分支，引入器官模式接口：使用稀疏Mixture-of-Experts（MoE）根据潜在放射学模式路由图像和文本令牌；可学习的槽位将路由后的令牌查询为连续的模式令牌；并通过配对的令牌对比学习，与从报告中提取的临床相似性构建的结构化软目标对齐。

Conclusion: OCP-CT通过引入器官条件下的放射学模式作为对齐单位，有效提升了CT视觉-语言预训练的精度与细粒度对齐能力，显著优于现有方法，在多个基准上取得了领先性能。

Abstract: Computed tomography (CT) vision-language pretraining from paired volumes and radiology reports is a scalable yet challenging task. Existing methods commonly adopt global scan-report contrast, which is scalable but obscures heterogeneous organ evidence. Meanwhile, direct organ-level alignment remains coarse, since the same anatomy can exhibit multiple distinct radiological appearances. Therefore, pretraining requires a finer alignment unit: the organ-conditioned radiological pattern. In this work, we propose OCP-CT, an organ-conditioned pattern-token alignment framework for CT vision-language pretraining. Specifically, OCP-CT preserves a stable global CT-report contrastive branch and introduces an organ pattern interface: sparse Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) routes image and text tokens according to latent radiological patterns, learnable slots query the routed tokens into continuous pattern tokens, and paired token contrast aligns image-text pattern tokens with structured soft targets built from report-derived clinical similarity. On the publicly available CT-RATE and RAD-ChestCT benchmarks, OCP-CT achieves average AUROCs of 84.5% and 69.9% for zero-shot abnormality diagnosis, respectively. Compared with the strongest prior reported results, these results yield absolute AUROC gains of 6.7 and 0.8 percentage points.

Abstract: The International StepUP Competition Series was launched to advance research in pressure-based footstep biometrics through a standardized and challenging evaluation framework. The competition attracted 26 registrants from academia and industry, with a best equal error rate of 8.00% achieved by the ArogyaPandit Research Team using a spatiotemporal CNN combined with an ensemble-based scoring strategy. ### [73] [Thresholded Cross-Attention for Reliable Intensity-Chromaticity Fusion in Low-Light Image Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13925)
*Yanyi Wu,Xu Zhang,Junkai Chen,Laibin Chang,Jiaqi Ma,Shi Chen,Linwei Zhu,Jianglei Di,Huan Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TCA-Net提出了一种基于阈值的交叉注意力机制，以实现低光照图像增强中强度与色度流的可靠融合。该方法通过自适应选择高置信度交互，克服了传统Top-K稀疏注意力在不同层间固定数量选择的局限性，并结合相位引导傅里叶交互模块和解耦双流引导模块，有效提升颜色保真度与结构一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于HVI的方法虽通过解耦强度与色度缓解颜色纠缠，但跨流融合的可靠性未被充分关注；发现跨流注意力置信度具有强层级依赖性，固定Top-K选择方式无法适配，导致部分层丢失有用信息，另一些层保留噪声。

Method: 提出TCA-Net，核心为阈值化交叉注意力（Thresholded Cross-Attention），用动态自适应的固定置信度阈值替代固定数量的Top-K选择，仅保留高置信度跨流交互；辅以相位引导傅里叶交互模块用于亮度初始化，解耦双流引导模块抑制色度泄漏，以及尺度感知一致性正则化增强对尺度扰动的鲁棒性。

Result: 在LOL-v1、LOL-v2、Sony-Total-Dark和LSRW-Huawei数据集上表现优异，兼具高恢复精度、良好颜色保真度与紧凑参数量，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: TCA-Net通过自适应可信度筛选实现更可靠的强度-色度融合，在保持高效的同时显著提升低光照图像增强质量，验证了注意力置信度建模在跨流融合中的关键作用。

Abstract: Low-Light Image Enhancement (LLIE) requires a careful balance among noise suppression, color fidelity, and efficiency. Recent HVI-based methods alleviate color entanglement by decoupling intensity and chromaticity, yet how reliably the two streams are fused again is an overlooked factor that largely determines the final quality. We observe that the confidence of cross-stream attention is strongly layer-dependent, so the fixed-quota selection of Top-K sparse attention is mismatched to it, discarding informative dependencies in some layers while retaining noisy ones in others. Motivated by this observation, we propose TCA-Net, a network built around Thresholded Cross-Attention that targets reliable intensity-chromaticity fusion in the HVI space rather than introducing yet another color representation. At its core, TCA replaces the rigid Top-K quota with a fixed confidence threshold whose retained cardinality is input- and layer-adaptive, retaining only high-confidence cross-stream interactions while suppressing unreliable ones. Around this core, two complementary designs clean up the fusion before and after it: a Phase-guided Fourier Interaction Module provides a structure-aware brightness initialization for the intensity stream prior to fusion, and a Decoupled Dual-Stream Guidance Module constructs residual intensity features to suppress chromaticity leakage during reconstruction. A Scale-Aware Consistency Regularization further improves structural robustness under scale perturbations during training. Extensive experiments on LOL-v1, LOL-v2, Sony-Total-Dark, and LSRW-Huawei demonstrate that TCA-Net delivers competitive restoration accuracy, improved color fidelity, and a compact parameter size.

</details>

*Thang-Anh-Quan Nguyen,Moussab Bennehar,Luis Guillermo Roldao Jimenez,Nathan Piasco,Dzmitry Tsishkou,Laurent Caraffa,Jean-Philippe Tarel,Roland Brémond*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖合成数据增强或物理模型，需要成对训练数据，难以生成真实天气效果且泛化能力差，因此亟需一种无需配对数据、能生成逼真且结构保持的多场景天气变化的新方法。

Method: 提出基于潜在扩散模型的Cyclone框架，结合循环一致性约束与图像-文本模型的知识，实现无监督的天气条件生成与编辑，支持跨场景、多天气类型的可控生成，并可通过蒸馏转化为视频扩散模型以保证时间一致性。

Result: 实验表明，Cyclone生成的天气效果更真实、结构保持更好，在多个下游驾驶感知任务中均带来稳定性能提升；其蒸馏后的视频版本也实现了良好的时序一致性。

Conclusion: Cyclone为自动驾驶中的天气鲁棒感知提供了一种高效、通用且无需配对数据的解决方案，具备强泛化能力和实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Reliable perception under diverse weather conditions remains a major challenge for autonomous driving systems. A common strategy to improve robustness is either to synthesize adverse weather conditions for training perception models or to apply weather-removal techniques to recover clean inputs. However, existing approaches typically rely on synthetic data augmentation or physics-based, task-specific models that require paired training data and often struggle to generate realistic weather effects or generalize robustly to out-of-domain scenarios. Toward this problem, we present Cyclone, a unified framework for weather editing based on latent diffusion, equipped with cycle-consistent constraints and knowledge from image-text models. Cyclone enables the generation of multiple weather conditions across diverse scenes while eliminating the need for paired data. Experimental results show that our approach produces more realistic, structure-preserving outputs than existing baselines and leads to consistent improvements across several downstream driving perception tasks. Furthermore, we demonstrate that Cyclone can be distilled to a video diffusion model for temporally consistent weather editing.

### [75] [SIVA-RL: Sensitivity-Invariance Visual Alignment for Multimodal Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13931)
*Cheng Tang,Junzhi Ning,Min Cen,Wei Li,Xinyi Zeng,Pinxian Zeng,Rongbin Li,Qiming Zhu,Yuqiang Li,Junjun He,Yirong Chen,Ming Hu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SIVA-RL提出一种新的视觉对齐框架，通过样本级、结果导向的监督机制替代传统基于操作符的正则化，利用局部化、距离受限的PatchSwap构建干预，并通过冻结审计策略评估奖励下降，实现敏感性与不变性对齐，显著提升多模态推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉干预方法依赖于干预类型进行监督，但相同操作在不同样本中效果不一，导致监督不可靠；需要一种更鲁棒、基于实际观测效果的监督方式以确保模型真正基于视觉证据进行推理。

Method: SIVA-RL采用令牌对齐、距离约束的图像内PatchSwap生成局部干预，通过冻结审计策略评估每对干净-干预图像的奖励下降，将奖励下降作为软路由权重：高下降对驱动敏感性对齐，低下降对驱动清洁锚定的不变性对齐，模糊对则降权处理，从而实现干预构造与监督分配解耦。

Result: 在九个涵盖数学、逻辑和视觉依赖任务的多模态推理基准上，SIVA-RL在3B和7B模型上均优于匹配的强化学习基线，在视觉依赖推理任务上提升8.79个百分点，整体相对提升最高达14.9%，适用于GRPO和DAPO两种骨干网络。

Conclusion: SIVA-RL通过结果导向的样本级监督机制，有效提升了视觉语言模型在多模态推理中的视觉证据对齐能力，显著增强了模型的可解释性与准确性，为强化学习中的可验证奖励设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) drives multimodal reasoning, but answer-level correctness does not guarantee that a vision-language model grounds its predictions in visual evidence. Existing visual-intervention methods contrast policy behavior on original and modified images, yet assign supervision by the type of intervention rather than its observed effect. This assumption fails: identical operators produce heterogeneous outcomes across samples. We propose SIVA-RL, a Sensitivity-Invariance Visual Alignment framework that replaces operator-conditioned regularization with sample-wise, outcome-conditioned supervision. SIVA-RL constructs localized interventions through token-aligned, distance-constrained within-image PatchSwap. A frozen audit policy then scores each clean-intervention pair, and the observed reward drop becomes soft routing weights. Large-drop pairs drive sensitivity alignment, low-drop pairs drive clean-anchored invariance alignment, and ambiguous pairs are down-weighted. This design decouples intervention construction from supervision assignment and is compatible with both GRPO and DAPO backbones. Across nine multimodal reasoning benchmarks spanning mathematical, logical, and vision-dependent tasks, SIVA-RL improves 3B and 7B models over matched RL baselines in every setting. It yields an 8.79 percentage-point gain on vision-dependent reasoning and up to 14.9% relative overall improvement across all four GRPO- and DAPO-based configurations.

Abstract: Arrhythmogenic left ventricular cardiomyopathy is a genetic myocardial disease difficult to diagnose due to the lack of gold standard criteria. Simultaneous PET/MR imaging, combined with multiparametric quantitative analysis, could facilitate the identification of different profiles related to the phenotype and progression of cardiomyopathy. This preliminary study focuses on a methodological strategy for dealing with PET/MRI data, including inter-patient data linkage and regional analysis. Two-step clustering was applied to T1 and T2 maps, LGE, and 18F-FDG-PET images of 99 patients genetically diagnosed with arrhythmogenic left ventricular cardiomyopathy. Thirty-two inter-patient groups of supervoxels were obtained by spectral clustering. They enabled the generation of automated textual and bullseye health reports for each patient, which were compared with cardiac imager assessments using balanced accuracy in repeated nested cross-validation. The reports generated by clustering accurately identified most of the cardiac physicians' observations (BA = 0.76 $\pm$ 0.04 in repeated nested cross-validation on patients, and BA $\ge$ 0.8 on phantoms). Furthermore, the identified abnormal clusters closely matched their visual observations, facilitating the identification of varying degrees of fibrosis or inflammation on the images. This approach enables a more systematic handling of multimodal PET/MRI data to characterise myocardial heterogeneity in arrhythmogenic left ventricular cardiomyopathy patients.

### [77] [Peak-End-Net: A Peak-End Rule Inspired Framework for Generalizable Video Aesthetic Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13941)
*Geng Li,Haiwen Li,Rui Chen,Jing Tang,Lei Sun,Xiangxiang Chu*

Main category: cs.CV

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频美学评估（VAA）因缺乏大规模基准数据集以及美学判断的高度主观性而进展缓慢。现有方法未能充分考虑人类对时间性体验的感知规律，尤其是'峰终定律'——人们主要根据体验中的显著时刻和结尾来评价整体感受。因此，亟需一种能反映人类心理感知规律的建模方法，以推动VAA的发展。

Method: 提出Peak-End-Net框架，其核心包括：1）通过预训练图像美学评估头生成帧级美学先验，用于定位美学显著时刻；2）设计美学节奏编码器，建模视频美学随时间的动态演化；3）引入动态门控融合机制，增强模型在分布偏移下的鲁棒性；4）基于冻结的视觉变压器（ViT），仅少量参数可训练，实现高效与可扩展性。

Result: 在两个主流VAA基准数据集VADB（域内评估）和DIVIDE-3K（跨域测试）上，Peak-End-Net均取得当前最佳性能，显著优于现有方法。实验表明，基于心理规律的建模有效提升了视频美学评估的准确性与可解释性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了将心理学原理如'峰终定律'融入视频美学评估建模的可行性与有效性。所提出的Peak-End-Net框架不仅性能优越，而且具有轻量化、可解释性强、参数效率高等优势，为未来视频理解任务中的人类感知建模提供了新思路。

Abstract: Video aesthetic assessment (VAA) aims to predict how aesthetically pleasing a video is, yet remains far less explored than other visual assessment tasks. Its progress is hindered not only by the scarcity of large-scale benchmarks, but also by the intrinsic subjectivity of aesthetic judgment, which is shaped by human perception. In this paper, we revisit VAA from a psychological perspective and propose \textit{Peak-End-Net}, a lightweight and interpretable framework inspired by the \textit{peak-end rule}, which suggests that people tend to judge a temporal experience mainly according to its salient moments and the ending. Building on this intuition, we first transfer knowledge from image aesthetic assessment (IAA) to VAA by introducing a pretrained IAA head to produce frame-wise aesthetic priors, which serve as surrogate signals for identifying aesthetically salient moments and guiding \textit{peak-end rule}-based temporal aggregation. To further capture how a video evolves aesthetically over time, we design an aesthetic rhythm encoder that models temporal progression beyond isolated moments. Additionally, we refine the overall assessment through a dynamic gated fusion mechanism to improve robustness under distribution shift. Our method is built on a frozen vision transformer (ViT) and requires only a small number of trainable parameters, making it scalable and parameter-efficient. Extensive experiments on two existing VAA benchmarks, including in-domain evaluation on VADB and cross-domain testing on DIVIDE-3K, demonstrate that our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance, affirming the value of psychologically grounded modeling for VAA. Our code and models are available at https://github.com/AMAP-ML/Peak-End-Net.

### [78] [PlumeQuant: Uncertainty-aware consistency assessment of methane plume masks and emission-rate estimates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13945)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用遗传算法（GA）生成多组满足发布参数（IME和泄漏长度）的合理掩膜，结合PlumeQuant工具重构所有物理量及不确定性；对比四种掩膜形式：原始参考掩膜、基于碳测绘启发的CM-like掩膜、GA集合掩膜及专家编辑掩膜，评估一致性与偏差。

Conclusion: 当前甲烷泄漏产品的标量参数不足以唯一确定泄漏边界，存在等效性问题。尽管产品整体一致性良好，但对弱或偏移泄漏仍具模糊性，需引入专家判断进行质量控制与审校。

Abstract: Imaging spectrometers increasingly distribute source-resolved methane plume products in which the plume mask, integrated mass enhancement (IME), plume length, emission rate, and uncertainty are physically and algorithmically linked. Using 63 EMIT-derived Carbon Mapper plume records from 27 scenes, we show that these published scalar quantities do not uniquely constrain the plume boundary: substantially different yet plausible masks reproduce the same IME, plume length, and emission rate. Genetic-algorithm (GA) ensembles conditioned on the published IME and plume length make this equifinality explicit: the high-confidence core selected by nearly all target-consistent masks covers a median of 13% of the plausible footprint envelope, and ambiguity is largest for weak, low-overlap plumes. The diagnostics come from PlumeQuant, which recomputes IME, plume length, emission rate, and five-term uncertainty from distributed product components under stated conventions and evaluates four mask representations: the distributed reference mask, a transparent Carbon Mapper-informed analogue (CM-like), the GA ensemble, and optional expert edits. The CM-like mask is generated per plume without access to the reference mask or published quantities, with settings fixed once on a scene-disjoint 44-plume development split. It reproduced published IME with +0.72% median difference and emission rate with +0.16% (6.98% mean absolute), reached 0.843 median intersection-over-union against the reference masks, and matched the published uncertainty scale (median ratio 1.01). Holdout mean absolute errors were 7.6% (IME), 9.5% (length), and 6.1% (rate). These are product-level consistency diagnostics, not independent validation. They flag weak, offset, or ambiguous plumes for expert review.

### [79] [CF-Net: Conflict Fusion with Speaker Normalisation and Certainty Weighting for Ambivalence/Hesitancy Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13976)
*Tung Hung Bui,Hong Hai Nguyen,Van Thong Huynh*

Result: 在 BAH 验证集上取得 0.7155 的宏平均 F1；在私有测试集上达到 0.7364 的 F1（AP = 0.7492），表现优于当前基准。

Abstract: Detecting ambivalence and hesitancy (AH) in unconstrained video is challenging because the target signal is inherently ambiguous and expressed through subtle cross-modal incongruence rather than prototypical affect. We present CF-Net, a deep multimodal network submitted to the 3rd Edition of the AH Video Recognition Challenge (ABAW 11th, ECCV 2026), targeting the BAH dataset. CF-Net encodes visual, audio, and transcript streams with frozen SigLIP2, HuBERT, and DistilBERT backbones, normalises backbone features per speaker to reduce identity leakage, and fuses them via a ConflictFusion module that explicitly computes pairwise cross-modal incongruence. CF-Net achieves a Macro F1 of 0.7155 on the BAH validation set and 0.7364 (AP = 0.7492) on the private challenge test set.

### [80] [Music-to-Dance Generation via Atomic Movements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13978)
*Xinhao Cai,Yixuan Sun,Minghang Zheng,Qingchao Chen,Xin Jin,Song-chun Zhu,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结构感知的音乐驱动舞蹈生成框架，将舞蹈建模为可解释的原子动作序列，通过大规模舞蹈数据分割与聚类，并利用大语言模型语义重标注构建可复用的原子动作词汇表。采用两阶段生成流程：先规划原子动作类型、时长和时间点，形成符号化舞蹈分配；再通过过渡感知生成器合成流畅且风格一致的动作。实验表明，该方法在结构连贯性、节奏对齐和感知自然度方面显著优于现有基线，同时具备更高的可解释性和可控编辑能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经方法将运动视为连续信号，忽视舞蹈的组成性，导致生成舞蹈结构不连贯且难以控制。因此需要一种能捕捉舞蹈结构性质的方法，以实现更合理、可解释的舞蹈生成。

Method: 首先对大规模舞蹈数据进行分割并聚类，形成原子动作组；接着使用大语言模型对聚类结果进行语义重标注与优化，得到可解释的原子动作词汇；设计两阶段生成框架：第一阶段基于音乐预测原子动作的类型、持续时间和时间安排，生成符号化舞蹈规划；第二阶段利用过渡感知生成器根据规划生成平滑、风格一致的运动序列。

Result: 所提方法在结构连贯性、节奏对齐和感知自然度上均显著优于现有基线；生成舞蹈具有更强的可解释性与可控编辑能力，支持用户对舞蹈结构进行显式调整。

Conclusion: 本文提出的结构感知框架有效捕捉了舞蹈的组成特性，通过原子动作建模与两阶段生成策略，实现了高质量、可控且语义清晰的音乐驱动舞蹈生成。该方法为舞蹈生成提供了新的结构化视角，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: Music-driven dance generation aims to produce human motion that is both rhythmically synchronized and semantically consistent with music. While recent neural approaches have achieved impressive visual realism, they typically model motion as a continuous signal and neglect its compositional nature, making generated dances structurally incoherent and difficult to control. In this work, we introduce a structure-aware framework that models choreography as a sequence of atomic movements-semantically interpretable motion events that serve as the building blocks of dance. To construct this atomic movement vocabulary, we first segment large-scale dance data and cluster them into atomic movement groups. We then employ a large language model to semantically relabel and refine the clusters, yielding a set of interpretable and reusable atomic movements. Based on these atomic movement annotations, we design a two-stage generation framework that mirrors the human choreography process. In the atomic movement planning stage, the model predicts the type, duration, and timing of atomic movements conditioned on the input music, forming a symbolic dance allocation. In the completion stage, a transition-aware generator synthesizes smooth and stylistically coherent motion conditioned on the planned structure. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method produces dances with significantly improved structural coherence, rhythmic alignment, and perceptual naturalness compared to existing baselines, while providing enhanced interpretability and controllable editing through explicit structural representation.

### [81] [Screening Is Effective for Visual Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13983)
*Shunya Shimomura,Kazuhiro Hotta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VisionScreen提出一种新的视觉模型，通过将语言建模中的Screening机制扩展到视觉识别任务中，解决ViT在处理图像块时难以独立评估相关性的局限。该方法基于查询-键相似性对二维空间中的图像块进行绝对相关性估计，并通过阈值筛选排除低相关性块，从而实现更精准的特征聚合。实验表明，VisionScreen在图像分类任务上优于传统ViT，验证了Screening机制在视觉领域的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ViT中的自注意力机制通过softmax归一化为所有图像块分配相对权重，无法独立评估各块的相关性，导致冗余或背景信息被引入特征聚合过程，影响性能。为此，需引入一种能独立判断块相关性并主动排除无关块的方法。

Method: 将语言模型中的Screening机制拓展至二维图像空间，将图像块视为网格排列的tokens，基于查询与键的相似性计算每个块的绝对相关性，并通过阈值筛选保留高相关性块，实现非竞争性、选择性特征聚合。

Result: 在多个图像分类基准测试中，VisionScreen表现优于标准ViT，证明其在提升特征表示质量与减少噪声干扰方面的有效性。

Conclusion: Screening机制可有效应用于视觉识别任务，提供一种替代传统softmax注意力的新型特征聚合方式，具备更高的灵活性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Vision Transformer (ViT) has been widely used as a powerful framework for modeling global dependencies among image patches. However, its core component, self-attention assigns softmax-normalized relative weights to all patches, making it difficult to evaluate the relevance between patches independently. In visual recognition, images often contain many background or redundant patches, yet self-attention cannot explicitly reject such irrelevant patches, which may introduce unnecessary information into feature aggregation. To address this limitation, Screening has been proposed in the field of language modeling, where the relevance of each token is independently evaluated based on query-key similarity and low-relevance tokens are explicitly excluded through thresholding. In this work, we propose VisionScreen, a new vision model that extends Screening mechanism to visual recognition. VisionScreen treats image patches as tokens arranged on a two-dimensional grid and extends absolute relevance estimation based on query-key similarity to the two-dimensional spatial domain. This allows each patch to selectively aggregate only content-wise and spatially relevant patches without relying on competition among patches. Experiments on image classification benchmarks demonstrate that the proposed method outperforms conventional ViT. These results suggest that Screening can be effective for visual recognition, offering an alternative to relative feature aggregation based on softmax attention.

</details>


### [82] [Task-Specific Feature Fusion Method for Multi-Task Affective Behavior Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13986)
*Jiajun Sun,Zhe Gao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究针对ABAW11多任务情感行为分析挑战，提出一种任务自适应的特征融合方法。通过在外部表情数据集上微调DINOv2 ViT-L和DINOv3 ConvNeXt-base模型，并冻结其权重提取帧级特征，系统比较了多种预测头、时序处理策略与融合机制。最终采用任务特定的融合与预测策略，而非统一架构，在验证集上取得EXPR宏F1 0.4222、AU宏F1 0.5402、VA均值CCC 0.6717，总分1.6341，表明该方法简单有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不同情感分析任务（如情绪、面部动作单元、唤醒度-效价）虽相关，但依赖不同的视觉特征、时序处理方式与融合策略，统一架构可能限制性能。因此需探索任务自适应的特征融合机制以提升多任务表现。

Method: 采用预训练视觉骨干网络DINOv2 ViT-L与DINOv3 ConvNeXt-base，在外部表情数据集上微调并冻结；从ABAW11数据中提取帧级特征；对比多种帧级预测头、时序卷积头、后处理平滑、LightGBM、特征拼接、门控融合、残差融合、晚期逻辑融合、阈值校准及共享多任务结构，最终选择任务特定的融合与预测策略。

Result: 在ABAW11验证集上，系统实现EXPR宏F1 0.4222，AU宏F1 0.5402，VA均值CCC 0.6717，综合得分1.6341，优于统一架构方案。

Conclusion: 任务自适应的冻结特征融合策略在ABAW风格的多任务情感行为分析中表现优异，无需强制所有任务共享同一架构即可实现高性能，证明该方法简洁且高效。

Abstract: The 11th Affective Behavior Analysis in-the-wild (ABAW11) Multi-Task Learning Challenge requires a unified system to predict valence-arousal, categorical expressions, and facial action units from the official s-Aff-Wild2 images. Although these tasks are naturally related through facial behavior, our validation experiments show that they benefit from different visual features, temporal processing strategies, fusion mechanisms, and calibration procedures. In this paper, we study task-adaptive feature fusion for ABAW11 multi-task affective behavior analysis. We first adapt two pretrained visual backbones, DINOv2 ViT-L and DINOv3 ConvNeXt-base, on an external expression-oriented facial image set and then freeze them to extract complementary frame-level features from the official ABAW11 data. On top of these frozen features, we systematically compare frame-level prediction heads, temporal convolutional heads, post-hoc temporal smoothing, LightGBM models, feature concatenation, gated fusion, residual fusion, late logit fusion, threshold calibration, and shared MTL structures. The final system selects task-specific fusion and prediction strategies rather than forcing all tasks to share a single architecture. On the ABAW11 validation set, the selected system achieves an EXPR macro-F1 of 0.4222, an AU macro-F1 of 0.5402, and a mean VA CCC of 0.6717, resulting in an overall validation score of 1.6341. The results suggest that task-adaptive fusion of frozen visual features is a simple and effective strategy for ABAW-style multi-task affective behavior analysis.

</details>


### [83] [M$^\text{4}$World: A Multi-view Multimodal Driving World Model for Interactive Object Manipulation and Minute-long Streaming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14005)
*Ke Cheng,Hanqiao Ye,Lei Shi,Yahui Liu,Yunhan Shen,Jingtao Dong,Zhenke Wang,Wenxuan Ao,Weixiang Xu,Kaining Huang,Shuhan Shen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: M$^\text{4}$World 是一个支持多视角、多模态生成的驾驶世界模型，能够合成未来的环绕视图视频流和同步的激光雷达扫描数据，并支持交互式物体操控与长达分钟级的稳定流式输出。通过灵活的条件控制接口实现细粒度物体操控，利用多阶段训练框架实现仅需四步去噪即可在线因果生成，保持长时间推演中的世界动态一致性。此外，引入高效的少量片段后训练方法及视觉参考条件生成模型，在保留通用生成能力的同时支持罕见场景定制化。为评估可控性，提出基于视觉语言模型的自动化评判流程，涵盖场景级条件遵循、视图间物体可控性与跨视图一致性。实验表明，M$^\text{4}$World 在生成质量、可控性和长期稳定性方面表现优异，适用于可控制、可扩展的自动驾驶仿真。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有驾驶世界生成方法在物体级可控性和长时序稳定性方面存在局限，难以满足自动驾驶仿真对精细控制和长时间稳定生成的需求。

Method: 提出 M$^\text{4}$World 模型，采用多阶段训练框架实现快速因果生成（仅四步去噪），结合灵活的条件接口支持空间布局与外观的显式控制；引入少量片段后训练和视觉参考条件生成模型以增强长尾场景的可控性；设计基于 VLM 的自动化评估流程，全面衡量生成质量与可控性。

Result: M$^\text{4}$World 实现了高保真生成质量、精确的物体级可控性以及稳定的分钟级流式输出；在下游任务如长尾数据增强和场景编辑中表现卓越，验证其在可控、可扩展驾驶仿真中的潜力。

Conclusion: M$^\text{4}$World 为自动驾驶仿真提供了强大的可控生成能力，具备高精度、长时稳定、多模态协同的特性，是迈向大规模、真实感、可干预仿真环境的关键进展。

Abstract: Driving-world generation has emerged as a core capability for scalable autonomous-driving simulation, yet existing methods remain limited in object-level controllability and long-horizon stability. We present M$^\text{4}$World, a Multi-view and Multimodal generative driving world model that synthesizes future surround-view video streams and synchronized LiDAR scans while supporting interactive object Manipulation and stable Minute-long streaming. Fine-grained object manipulation is realized through a flexible conditioning interface that supports explicit control over both the spatial layout and visual appearance of individual objects. Stable minute-long streaming, on the other hand, is achieved through a multi-stage training framework that enables online causal generation in only four denoising steps while maintaining coherent world dynamics throughout extended rollouts. Building on these components, we introduce an efficient few-clip post-training as well as a suite of visual reference-conditioned generation models, preserving general generation ability while allowing rare-case customization for long-tail controllability. To assess controllability beyond realism, we further introduce an automated VLM-based judging pipeline that evaluates scene-level condition adherence, view-wise object controllability, and cross-view object consistency. Comprehensive experiments show that M$^\text{4}$World consistently delivers high generation quality, precise controllability, and stable minute-long streaming. Together with downstream long-tail augmentation and scene editing, these results demonstrate the potential of M$^\text{4}$World for controllable, scalable driving simulation.
